Selected Speeches of Reverend Sun Myung Moon
340
Compiled by the Editorial Committee for Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Speeches

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Reverend Sun Myung Moon, who received the calling for the salvation of humanity from Heaven at the age of 16, has lived his life centered solely on the Heavenly Way. He described his life as follows:
"If Reverend Moon has any wealth, it is the suffering endured for the public rather than for myself, and that is all the wealth I have. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. From a providential standpoint, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. …… Reverend Moon has faced countless opposition and persecution from the nation and the world. I was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communism. Never in history has the world united to attack and eliminate one person as they have with me. In that sense, I might be a world champion.
However, despite being criticized, I have not been destroyed or ruined. I have emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. …… Reverend Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the spirit world, hell, and even God.” (Refer to the Collection of Speeches, Volume 105, pages 101-103)
In short, Reverend Moon's life is 'suffering itself.' This suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. Here, we come to know who he is. Reverend Moon is the Messiah and Savior that Christianity has hoped for over 2000 years, and he has come as the True Parent of humanity. Already, in 185 countries worldwide, disciples following Reverend Moon are realizing the ideal of the True Family to walk the path of true children with such a confession of faith.
Reverend Moon's identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humanity, history and the world, are clarified through his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled in him, setting us free. These words contain 'vitality.' Moreover, the more important point is that Reverend Moon's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, or incarnated. Therefore, life itself is the truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'the Word.'
I am confident that readers will understand his greatness through Reverend Moon's words. The level of Reverend Moon's words is so high and deep that it cannot be fully comprehended, but fundamentally, it has three characteristics.
First, Reverend Moon revealed God through his words and life. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the lineage of evil, God's pain is that of having children who cannot be called children. Reverend Moon made the sorrowful God, who was tragically alienated by human sin, 'speak.' He made the silent God, trapped in doctrines and ornate buildings, 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as a parent, 'become a parent,' thus Reverend Moon is 'the complete revelation of God.'
Secondly, Reverend Moon liberated humans from ignorance and chaos. Although we humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, we cannot deny the tragic reality that we cannot fully explain our own existence. Moreover, although humans are not independent beings but interdependent with others, we have not been able to clarify that relationship. The reason is that we lost God's words. In response, Reverend Moon provides the ultimate answer. Furthermore, through a life that upholds the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete exemplary path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, Reverend Moon liberated the world of all things. Every creation made by God has its own unique value as an individual truth body. Although its value should be fully realized under the original dominion of a true human, it has not been, and thus all things have groaned. Reverend Moon clarified the original value of the world of all things through his words and opened the way for the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Reverend Moon and his wife, who have come as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly speak around the world today, demonstrating through their substantial lives the teachings of 'Serve with the heart of a parent and the body of a servant' and 'Live for the sake of others,' striving to bequeath true love, true life, and true lineage.
Additionally, through his words of life, noble life, and achievements, Reverend Moon has finally restored God's kingship as we welcome the new millennium, settling as the King of Blessed Families on this earth. He has established the Peace UN, binding the world into one realm of heart, aiming for the Kingdom of Peace, Cheon Il Guk, and the Fourth Israel.
I hope that the readers who encounter these words will become owners of Cheon Il Guk and play a leading role in building the Kingdom of Peace. *

10   The Model of the Owner of Love in Eight Stages
The entire universe, which God moves, is designed to live following the air of love. Without air, there is no existence, so one must do everything possible to follow where air is. That is the world. Do you understand? "Yes."
Whenever there is difficulty in life, when you have to decide whether to go left or right at a horizontal standard that can overcome the ridge of death, you must go right. How much have you been indebted to the universe? Isn't that right?
From every creature and plant, from elements, you have absorbed everything unconditionally to compose your body and received it without cost. After growing and living, where do you go? You head towards a greater world without cost, towards the infinite God Himself, where your entire existence can harmonize with all living emotions and the unified realm of love. (The recording is briefly interrupted)
Money, knowledge, and power have nothing to do with it. You were not born for them. They are auxiliary conditions for our human life. You must be able to give and receive the elemental love. From a child, everything must be given and received.
Therefore, when you think about the fact that you are an entity that has received infinite benefits from the universe, how will you repay it? When the received entity goes to the great owner, a normal cycle occurs. Small things must return as small. They must cycle. Large things must cycle as large. They must connect to something greater. The ultimate greater one is God, so you enter the realm of oneness with love centered on God. You return to God. Do you understand what I mean? You must know this amazing fact of life.
11 
Therefore, how should you die? You should not die in a luxurious house with your friends and children. If you die while trying to save the place where your brothers are groaning in life and death, you become a representative that all brothers can commemorate, leaving a historical tradition before the world.
Glory is something that can be welcomed by the world
A person who dies for themselves is not acceptable. That is a shadowy group. If you die for heaven and earth, for God, you become light, light. You become light.
Without the concept of love, light…. Isn't that what light is? What is glory? Is it glory to live well alone? What is it to enjoy the wealth and honor of the world? Living in harmony with the upper, lower, left, right, front, back, even with the people, the nation, and the world, in a position where you can be welcomed, is glory, glory.
Isn't that right? Glory (榮光) means everything is balanced. The character '榮' includes 'fire 火' twice, 'roof 宀,' and 'tree 木.' It includes trees, houses, fire, and light. It speaks of glory. It is used from a subject position when you can give to the whole because you have received and can breathe comfortably. Cells must all take balance and move in a sine curve according to that frequency. The frequency is high, but even if the form is small, it must enter that form.
12   The Model of the Owner of Love in Eight Stages
Electricity is the same. It is three-phase, three-phase. It has three loops. One goes like this, this goes in the middle, and another goes like this. These three are connected and come out, so when electricity is cut off, it flickers. It happens because it flows quickly, appearing as a line. The eyes have an error. It is three-phase.
When you see this, the universe is made according to the number three, like the three primary colors, three nutrients. This is also three stages. This (mouth) speaks of the world of water. Do you drink water through here? Rice is also water. More than 60 percent of rice is water. What is this? Do you drink water through here? The water era is necessary, the water era. This is the water era, so it must be below, and air is the middle era. This speaks of the era of love. The eyes speak of the highest. Because of the eyes, the head turns. Because of love, because of ideals, everything moves. This (ears) speaks of the four directions, the four directions.
All the five senses are where? The hands are also the five senses. Where there is flesh, it is the five senses. It knows all the sensations, and this is the information center. It hears, sees, smells, and tastes. It is an information center. Therefore, it is designed for everything to live without feeling conflict, to be harmonious, and to live without any flaws. If it is a soccer ball, there is no dent. If there is a dent, it will go here and there while moving.
Therefore, when you look at the human body, the three stages are all there, aren't they? Now, read.
It is so detailed. So, when you go to the spirit world and want to come down, those with a strong heart of love can go anywhere. They can help anywhere. It means they can connect with high places. When you know such a principle, when you realize that the natural phenomenon world is connected in such a way, living while ignoring the environmental phenomenon realm is like cutting off your own legs and peeling off your shell. You must harmonize.
Try breathing deeply three times continuously. Can you just inhale? If you inhale ten times and do it once, you will die. Will you shrink or grow? It's the same. Everything must be relative. It is giving and receiving. Since you have received from the universe, you must give. In giving, you try to give something more valuable. That is giving for love. You must know that it is precious.
During your lifetime, you have received the elements of life from the universe and established the tradition of love, and you must repay all the universe, the source, for what you have received. In repaying, at what position do you repay? When you decide to repay even while suffering, that is the end, the end. At the end, you cannot return. You must decide to repay even if you die, and then you complete the path of day and night. When you form a sphere, half of it is always bright, and half is dark, isn't it? It's the same. You must walk the path of life that can overcome death to complete the path of day and night.
Therefore, in the Unification Church, there is a saying that the polluted bloodline must be cut, but the natural principle is the same. If there is day, there must be night. Isn't that right? Therefore, those who like the day alone cannot do it. If there is day, you must long for the night, and if there is night, you must long for the day. It is the same.
The path of love is one path
All these things have been taught in detail, but if you live knowing them as public opinion and pass away, consider it. If there is a ladder and you cannot take the elevator to a high-rise building, you must climb the stairs even if your legs hurt. As you go up, it becomes more frightening and dizzy. If there are wind walls, you may not know, but if you look down from the ladder, you feel like you will fall. But think about climbing because the ladder is connected. Without deciding to die, you cannot climb. It is the same. You must know that you are walking such a path.
So, weigh it and go. You must settle how you lived today and go. There is no one as foolish and stupid as someone with selfish desires. It is like sewing yourself backward. Individualism is destruction. It cannot avoid destruction. Heaven is also a negative place, hell. If you live for yourself. All things in the world have various shapes, but they exist to harmonize in the relationship between subject and object, as a glue to harmonize, as cement to harmonize. Nothing exists for itself. Everything exists to harmonize and unite, possessing relative and mediating conditions, so nothing can be missing.
You might say, 'Oh, why did God create snakes and such things?' but imagine if there were no lice. Many people survive in the desperate situation because lice bite them. Because lice bite, they suffer and scratch, and while scratching, they avoid being beheaded by the People's Army at the outpost.
It's the same in prison. Lice and bedbugs are friends. If you start catching lice in the morning, it takes 4 to 5 hours until lunchtime, and there are still lice. You don't feel hungry because of the fun of catching them. Bedbugs are the same. Bedbugs are friends, and fleas are friends. Even flies are friends. Who would you associate with? They become friends.
So, would you make friends with the vast, boundless world, or with dung flies, maggots? You can only be friends with dung flies. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."
Your mind should be able to fly from the East to the West several times a day, with a deep heart. Isn't that how your hometown is? It should be. If you lose your country, how much do you long for it? You must long for it more than eating, more than sleeping, more than living. You have lost everything. You have lost your parents, your hometown, and you have become a miserable being, but there is only one path to finding it, not two. Isn't that right? Is the path of love two paths or one path? "One path." It is absolutely one path. Finding that one path is the path to love your parents, and for parents to love their children. It is the path of filial piety in the family, the path of patriotism centered on the nation, the path of saints who can love the world, and the path of holy sons who can love the cosmos. This is an inevitable interconnected relationship in theoretical standards.
Are the eyes separate? Are the eyes separate? If there are eyes, but the nose does not breathe, what happens? If you do not breathe, what happens? Do the eyes close or not? "They close." What happens if you do not eat? What happens if you do not hear? Everything is to protect me. Everything is united to protect the common ownership. It is interconnected. You must know this.
Therefore, there is nothing to disregard. There is nothing unnecessary. It is absolutely necessary. It is not just the eyes that are necessary. If there are no nails, how do you scratch where it itches? It is a grateful thing when you think about it.
Unification Church members must treat senile ancestors well
Therefore, the universe protects me, so when I am hungry, I am hungry, and when I am sick, I take medicine. Do young people eat porridge or stronger rice when they are old? "Porridge." That is it. Are there any young people who would like to eat porridge? That child is not a young person.
The older you get, the more your wisdom declines. When wisdom declines, what remains is love. They only know eating, loving, and sleeping.
Look, old people only think about eating, right? Then they think about love, love. They think about love, but their physiological organs are all paralyzed. Eventually, they forget even love. When they become senile, they forget their mother, their son, everything, right? How could they go to the spirit world if they do not forget everything? They must forget everything and go.
When a baby is born, it breaks open its house, tears everything apart, and forgets it all. If it wanted to return, what would happen? It is the same. When leaving this world, you must forget everything and go. If you say, 'Oh, I don't want to go. Oh, I miss my father, I miss my grandson,' what would happen?
Therefore, how grateful is senility? Meanwhile, ancestors appear. What was seen vaguely in the fog of the distant world gradually appears before your eyes, entering the intermediate world, meeting all unseen ancestors, and seeing the lion or whoever comes to find you, connecting with another world. Forgetting is necessary to go on the path of greater knowledge. Therefore, those who despise senile grandparents lose the blessing of that family.
Unification Church members must treat senile ancestors well, not carelessly. "We must treat them well." True filial piety is in such positions, and true loyalty is in such positions. Those who pledge to walk the path of suffering for the king, for God, by offering their lives become central figures. They inherit the mainstream tradition of love. Therefore, you must become a filial child.
A filial child must overcome life. It is the same for loyal subjects. The path of a patriot is to die on behalf of the life of 40 million people if it is 40 million. The path of a saint is to go on behalf of the life and death of the 60 billion people of the world. The path of a holy son is to take responsibility for the life and death of the cosmos, which is in the billions. 
If there are two, you must think of dying first. If there are ten brothers, the one who goes first to die for the parents is the true filial child. A loyal subject is the one who goes first to the place of death among 40 million.
The body is a protective material for the spirit body
When it was said to offer all living things, people lied and fought over material things. Before Peter, Ananias and his wife sold their property and offered it, but when they offered half, they were buried on the spot. Do you know that? It is in the Bible, isn't it? Ananias and his wife…. It is the same.
What is precious about it? It is like maggots. It is a candidate for dung that is not yet in the stomach. Dung is not hateful. It is the residue squeezed out after providing nutrients to keep me alive. Is urine the enemy, or is dung the enemy? How much did it go through for me? It provided the nutrients to maintain my health and is the leftover. It is the shell that contained it. When a baby is in the womb, it breaks through and forgets everything, and the umbilical cord should be dried and given as a gift of love from the mother when the child grows up. It is precious. It is the precious thing that guaranteed safety for ten months.
The body is the same. It is the precious protective material that protected me throughout my life and blocked all difficult paths that could have harmed the spirit body.
Therefore, the blessed family is always at the original site, even if they are not at the church. Because the protective body that protected them is there, the closest person is there. Living is to repay what you owe. You must be the highest horizontal line. Entering the highest horizontal position of water is being born as a healthy baby from the womb world, and you must cross that ridge. You must destroy it. How difficult is it to destroy it? The mother must struggle, and the baby must use all its strength to destroy it. The protective pouch that protects the baby's life, like a vinyl that cannot be easily cut, must be strong. It bursts out with all its might. It is the same with the body. Because it is the armored protective skin that protected me for eighty years, no one can kill it recklessly.
That's it. They say you have to use all your strength, even from when you were a child, when you die, right? That's true. You have to burst out strongly. 
When you are born into the world of love, there is no way to burst it out. 
Can you push God aside and go somewhere else? No matter how much you go, no matter how much you run out, you are still within God's embrace. You cannot burst it out. You can never, ever burst it out. That is the greatest liberation. The environment and conditions that can relate to that world are infinite. It's infinite. It's an unimaginable infinite space. 
Do you want to go to that world? 
When you live in Korea and go abroad, you boast about having been to Japan and how much you've traveled around the world. Isn't talking about fishing in the five oceans, bathing somewhere, and going on tours all boasting? They are all gifts given to me. They are gifts. 
You have to know that you are living in a mission of love, where you can love freely and live freely. 
20 The Model of the Owner of Eight Stages of Love
So, if I have received everything from the universe and owe everything to the universe, shouldn't I pay it back? Isn't that right? When you pay it back with love, even a small gift from great parents' love is treated as something that represents the whole. 
That's what a gift is. With a small thing centered on a heart of love, you are filling it as something that can represent the whole. 
So, there is no concept centered on oneself that can receive and give. There is a way to give and receive centered on the concept of the subject centered on the counterpart. In that, there is no existence of oneself. 
Otherwise, the movement stops. When you forget and give more to give something bigger, it gradually grows. I have done this much. The teacher has lived like that all his life. If I had set something like that, I wouldn't have been able to do global work until now. What is the Pacific Rim providence these days? Since it came from water, it has to pass through the water nest centered on water. All the land is also twin continents, Asia, and the North and South continents. Centered on Hawaii, centered on the island, where should it be born? It should be born on land. In the buffer zone here, centered on Japan and the United States, the mother and the eldest son must become one, but who? The father has to do it. So, the ocean must be liberated. 
You have to give birth to two sons and daughters in the womb. That's right. 
The deepest part of the Pacific Ocean is over 10,000 meters, 10,132 meters. It's near the Philippines, they say. And the corner area is 6,000 meters. It's a relative relationship. The water flows through it all. That's why if you put all the mountain ranges on the land into the sea, would only seawater remain, or would you see land? "You would see land." Even if there is land, it came out from the water. It has to be like that. 
So, they are beings floating on water. There, animals and plants all correspond to each other, forming the shape of the universe, and the ideal stage of life is the earthly world. The spirit world is the same. There are no borders there. There are no distinctions like English people or American people. Here, English people and American people are different, right? Eastern people and Western people are different, right? There are no such things in the spirit world. Eastern people and anyone are all brothers.

What happens if you take one step there? You fall and get smashed to pieces, right? The first thing that hits gets smashed. Think about how serious it was for the teacher to come this far. That's why, no matter what tempts you in the world, you have to break through that temptation, nail it to God's chest, and climb up with a rope. What did I say now? What did I nail to God's chest? You have to nail it firmly and climb up so that it doesn't get pulled out. 
That's why when you pull it, if God has flesh, it gets pulled from the skin, from the flesh, from the bones, and even from the marrow. You have to lay such a ladder. Do you think it will be as easy as sitting here and thinking? It's a struggle, a struggle.

We must hold the Enthronement Ceremony for God's Kingship
You have to know yourself. How deep is this root? There are two roots. There are fake roots and real roots. When you pray sincerely, analyze yourself as if you are spreading out flat. What can you give to the Father, and where can you stand? Even if you research for a thousand years, it's not enough. 
That's why the teacher doesn't want to go to high places. There are children in prison and in hell, so how can a father and mother go to a good place and receive glorious blessings? Long life? That's the talk of crazy people. They are all trying to set up a ladder to get free things. 
Now, knowing that.... The year 2000 is passing. As we start anew in 3000, we must enthrone God. We must hold the Enthronement Ceremony. Who will do it? The True Parents. It is the Alpha and Omega. What makes this possible is true love. Just as children born in the world return to their mother and father.』
Therefore, even God absolutely obeys what? It is not knowledge, not money, not power, but true love. Isn’t it the same for men? They obey true love, right? It’s the same for women. No matter how great they are, it’s like that.
Even though God is absolute, He is only absolute in all aspects when He serves true love as the subject. Without true love, He is only half. Even God cannot help but obey true love.
Therefore, God cannot do as He pleases. If He could do as He pleases, why can’t He do as He pleases with the world? Through the path of love, He can govern everything, but God, who has not found His partner of love, is in a position where He cannot do as He pleases for a thousand or ten thousand years.
He would exercise the greatest absolute authority with true love, but He cannot because there is no true love. There is a path that He must go as the principled subject of true love, but He cannot go because there is no true love. He has not even started. Therefore, since the fall, God has been imprisoned. Do you understand what I’m saying? The absolute God has become a powerless God. Not only powerless, but He is lamenting. Isn’t that so?
If He cannot find the lost love, He remains a pitiful being, lamenting and creating a history of resentment. How can we relieve that resentment? Because the resentment is due to true love, we must relieve it with true love.
Without the true love that loves even enemies, we cannot liberate God
So, what is true love? It is to serve, invest, and forget. Therefore, you must love even your enemies. How absurd is that? The entire universe has become an enemy within Satan’s realm. Even though it was created with the ideal of love and as an element of love, due to the fall, it has become an element of resentment.
To digest such an element of resentment, God stands at the center of the process of re-creation. You must know how sorrowful and how absurdly God is suffering in such a situation. The fact that you stand in the providence of salvation with His cooperation…. God stands at the peak of resentment.
When you realize this, you must liberate Him with true love. With what? With knowledge? With power? With money? Only greater love, only a love that serves more, can make it possible. That is logical. You must appear with absolute love that serves more.
Therefore, when you think of God as your Father, you weep. When a beloved husband is lost, doesn’t the wife weep? Even if it is the child, the parents weep, and even if it is the parents, the child weeps. You must stand at the peak of weeping, shedding tears without knowing you are shedding tears, to the point of dying. You must shed tears with all your might, forgetting that you are shedding tears, to the point of dying, to turn God around and start the path of filial piety and loyalty that God seeks. Do you understand what I’m saying? That is logical. It is not a delusion.
What is God’s resentment? The absolute, unique, unchanging, and eternal God cannot have absolute authority. Why? He can have everything else, but He cannot have true love. What can comfort parents who have lost their child? Can money, knowledge, or a nation do it? When the value of a child that surpasses that is found, when the child thought dead is said to be alive, how would it be? Would you want to fly, or would you want to run?「I would want to fly.」You would want to fly. There is nothing faster or higher than that.
Therefore, even fallen humans must love and live for God to live. Tied to such a connection, who will untie it? It cannot be done without true love. Without the heart to love even enemies, it cannot be. You cannot start the theoretical system.
We must liberate God, who is obsessed with true love, from all existence
So, think from that perspective. Suppose you once lost someone you truly loved to an enemy. You appointed them as the queen when you were in the position of a king, but the country was destroyed, and the person who could have been the queen became the queen of the enemy country. Can that queen be happy, and can the person who lost that queen be happy? No matter how many flowers bloom and how full of fragrance that world is, what use is it, and what use is that joyful environment? It is all a condition of resentment. The flowers, the fragrance, they all bind and prick you. Isn’t that so? It is not abstract. It is a fact.
Therefore, God has no way out except to love His enemies. By loving His enemies, and by digesting the paradoxical path that God took to find them, a love that surpasses that must start to create a path to find God’s sons and daughters. It creates a path to find what was stolen from God’s bosom of love. Isn’t that so?
Unless you stand in the position of repenting for your sins, weeping and being thankful even if you die a thousand or ten thousand times, you cannot find the original standard of love, and you cannot erase the blemish of the history of resentment. Have you ever thought of such a thing?
God is obsessed with true love. He is hanging by the neck. All existence, all creation must untie that. The providence of salvation was carried out with only the heart to love His enemies. If that is removed, the chain of history is cut, and a knot is created. How absurd must it be for God, who must continue to have such a heart?
Even if you mourn for years over a lost wife, husband, or child, you cannot reach God’s heart. With the feelings of the fallen world, you cannot reach it. You cannot rise above the position of an archangel who received the bloodline of the fall.
For God to hold an enthronement ceremony, He must weave from all creation, from the angelic world, the satanic world, the enemy world, and the world of all things. He must liberate the God of resentment who has gone through such a process. The True Parents must liberate what the false parents brought down with such a heart.
These days, my heart is filled with nothing but that thought. There is no room to think about going to Jeju Island with Mother for a breeze. Is such a thing real or not? It is not a thought. I must find a position where I can act without even knowing it.
To hold the enthronement ceremony of God’s kingship
So, from the smallest animal to the entire world of creation, then the angelic world, and the world of Adam, everything has collapsed. If it took hundreds or thousands of years to wait, you must compress that waiting and say it was done in an instant with the center of love. Without such a heart, you cannot think of liberating God.
God lost His kingship, but to hold the enthronement ceremony…. Think about it. No matter how much I suffer throughout my life, it is not a problem. How I conduct that ceremony is a big task.
So, more than God’s love for saving the enemy of enemies, more than God’s love for Satan, the problem is which son can comfort God. What kind of filial son, the entity that will inherit God’s body, is that entity? You must go beyond that realm. You must go beyond that realm to hold the enthronement ceremony of God’s kingship. How serious is that?
Do you understand how terrifying the term ‘registration ceremony’ is? It is a responsibility taken by me and Heung-jin. All the responsibilities taken before God become conditions for saying, ‘I want to do this.’ ‘Go ahead,’ He will say. It is all about taking responsibility. Do you understand what I’m saying?
Just as God came with the heart to make Satan’s son His son, the registration ceremony is about taking responsibility for the entire ideal. The True Parents on earth and Heung-jin…. If Heung-jin alone cannot do it, even the four children must be divided and take responsibility.
The four great saints were included in that. What must be connected here are the twelve people, if twelve, or 72 disciples, if 72, or 120 disciples, if 120, established by the saints in the religious sects. In the era of the apostles, it is 160 families to 180 families.
Even if you could burn the enemy at once, the heart to love and forget the resentment and bitterness must come first. It is not imagination. You must enter the realm of substance and find the path. Is it serious or not?「It is serious.」It is different from the era of seeking truth. It is different from fighting with the knowledge of the will.
How will you solve the fundamental problem? How will you create God’s movement that can stand in a position beyond all indemnity and what you desire? Isn’t that the position where you can enthrone God?
So, what is there in front of a teacher who thinks like that? There is nothing. There is nothing like me, the UN, or anything else. The condition of having loved is praised by God, and He sets His heart anew, turning the heart of hell into God’s heart by several tens of times. If you cannot give such a shock, you cannot enthrone God.
So, when you look at it, the person called True Parents is the most pitiful person. There is nothing to boast about. Do you understand what I’m saying? Think about it. Now! (Continued reading)
Who will pray? Hwang Sun-jo, pray. (Hwang Sun-jo, President, prays) *

About the prayer meeting for the inauguration of the President of the United States
<Prayer> Loving Father, today is December 28, 2000, the day when Hyo-jin was born on this earth, marking the full 38th year, and by Korean age, the day he crosses the 40th milestone.
We know well how much he has suffered, being born as the eldest son in the True Parents’ family and having to overcome many emotional hurdles while walking a lonely path through difficult circumstances.
We also realize that heaven did not have the joy to protect him and the spirit world could not provide a protective environment, and now that he has reached the age of 40 by Korean age, let him use this birthday as a condition to realize what kind of parents he has, understand the path they have walked, and repent for all the past history that could not unite with heaven.
As we enter this new era of 2000, where forgiveness can be granted, bless him to become a son who can joyfully welcome God’s enthronement ceremony, and bless even the children of his family, we earnestly pray.
Now, as Yeon-ah takes on the dual responsibility of being the mother of those children, allow her to stand as a mother, and let him, as a father, not be ashamed on earth, and be able to gather and offer all historical things to heaven, as representatives of the parents.
Now, let the victorious world of heaven shine beyond the Korean people and the Moon clan, and allow the family to be a model for all registered children and families beyond the four-position foundation, and let them become sons who can be proud as the second generation of the Unification family, knowing that this is the desire of the True Parents, heaven, and all the blessed families in the spirit world.
We pray that you will protect and guide them so that they can walk the path they choose, leaving a path that can be a model for their children and future generations, and a path that can be a model for their wives.
For all the children gathered here to celebrate and those around the world who remember this day in their hearts, and for all the people who look at the calendar made centering on the True Parents, let them know what this day is, and for all the first and second generation blessed families who pray for this day, let heaven’s infinite blessings come without being a shadow or a blemish.
May the Father personally be with all of them on this day. For the family members remaining in East Garden and the remaining children in Boston, may heaven’s blessings be with them, and may the path they walk in the future be a path of victory, a path of pride for the filial son, Hyo-jin, we ask.
As we rejoice together on this day, may the glory and grace of the Father be with us forever. We pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen! Amen! Amen!

Prayer for the Inauguration of the President of the United States
The conscience is ahead of parents, teachers, and masters

If we explain about the conscience, the conscience is ahead of parents, ahead of teachers, and ahead of God. The conscience is not a part of God because it is centered on the representative standard of personality and dignity. The attributes are different from God. Therefore, what makes the different positions of husband and wife, man and woman, one? It is love.

God and humans can also become one through love. It is not a part of God. If it were a part, there would be no ideal in the unity. Since the wife is a different personality in front of the husband, there must be love to become one. Only true love can connect it.

What is love? We must logically explain that our body and mind are also connected by true love. Based on that result, we can establish the logic of the unity of heaven and earth, which liberates paradise and hell. We must include that briefly and talk about it.

"Are you saying to include the conscience here?" We must teach why the body and mind are divided. There is a lot written about the conscience, isn't there? It's okay to leave out all the explanations. The conscience is ahead of the teacher, ahead of the parents, and ahead of the king. In front of God, Adam and Eve are different masters, and because they are different masters, God cannot do as He pleases, so He invested the complete internal nature centered on the whole instead of God, which is the conscience.

Therefore, all personalities and individualities are different, and all consciences are different. The absolute standard of those differences is that the conscience is ahead of parents. Parents can separate when they marry, friends can separate, and everything can separate, but the conscience has been there since before one was born. Therefore, it cannot separate. It cannot separate forever with the conscience. So it is ahead of parents.

Isn't it the same with teachers? You learn, but what you have learned cannot guide you beyond the position of the conscience. However, the conscience guides me from the highest position. So, if you make a small mistake, the conscience feels guilty, doesn't it? It tells you not to do it.

Next, it is better than the master. It is better than God and better than the king. God is a separate personality, so He cannot come in and interfere. But this (conscience) comes in completely and teaches the master's position forever, and at the same time, it keeps the king's position so that one can bear the responsibility of the past, present, and future of one's duties.

Therefore, right after the fall, God, knowing everything, asked, "Adam! Where are you?" He asked Adam where he was. If it were a part, there would be no need to ask. Isn't that right? Because Adam, who has a conscience set on such a standard, is a different personality, God had to ask.

Even God absolutely obeys true love

Then who knew about the fall first, God or Adam? How would you answer? You cannot say God knew first. Adam and Eve knew because they experienced the suffering of the fall before God did. If God had known before, it would not have been a different personality.

Therefore, as a masculine subject, God, who is a different personality with a relative standard, hoped that Adam and Eve would be better than Himself centered on true love. If there is a husband and wife, the husband hopes that the wife is better than himself. He also hopes that the children are better. Because they are different love partners, he hopes for that. Isn't that right?

A love partner hopes that the partner becomes several tens of millions of times better than oneself. If it were the same body (part), there would be no need to hope for that. He hopes that they reach the highest peak. He hopes that they occupy the highest position. Then, he can rise together with them.

The body and mind can become one through love. Although there are differences in heaven and earth, by becoming one with the subject centered on true love, it becomes equalized. Only love can make equalization possible.

Therefore, even the absolute God absolutely obeys true love. Absolute obedience is hoping that it appears as the subject of infinite absolute value, the subject of infinite absolute love. The highest desire of love is to hope for a standard where there is nothing beyond it, even after a thousand or ten thousand years. So, it is called the ideal type for individuals. That is the relative relationship.

You can just put in the framework and connect it. There is no need to add anything else. They must listen and go back to study. We distribute books, don't we? "Yes." You can just tell them to refer to certain pages in the book. Do you understand? "Since it is a declarative statement to those people...."

Since the start of love was wrong, it must be corrected through blessing

Yes, just reading that, what universal story... Where does the true family come from? The world, heaven, and earth were all divided due to the struggle of the body and mind, but why were they divided? They were divided because of love. From the fallen position centered on false love... Because it was stronger than the power of the conscience at the time of the fall, if you think about the physical self at the end, you inevitably fall into hedonism and destructive tendencies, and you cannot help but fall into hell. It is the opposite of God, so it becomes like that.

No matter how great America is, no matter how great the Anglo-Saxons are, if they do not reverse the collapse caused by the wrong marriage of the ancestors of humanity who received God's direct lineage, there is no way to return. Therefore, the Unification Church is conducting re-blessing.
